result\n233\t}\n234\t\n235\t/// Render content with code block detection for Markdown\n236\tfn render_content_markdown(content: &str) -> String {\n237\t    // For Markdown, we mostly preserve the        parts.push(format!(\"{}h\", duration.num_hours() % 24));\n254\t    }\n255\t    if duration.num_minutes() % 60 > 0 {\n256\t        parts.push(format!(\"{}m\", duration.num_minutes() % 60));\n257\t    }\n258\t\n259\t    if parts.is_empty() {\n260\t        \"<1m\".to_string()\n261\t    } else {\n262\t        parts.join(\" \")\n263\t    }\n264\t}\n265\t\n266\t/// Format model(s) Role::ToolResult => \"Result\",\n284\t    }\n285\t}\n286\t\n287\t/// Escape HTML special characters\n288\tfn escape_html(s: &str) -> String {\n289\t    let mut result =          '>' => result.push_str(\"&gt;\"),\n295\t            '\"' => result.push_str(\"&quot;\"),\n296\t            '\\'' => result.push_str(\"&#x27;\"),\n297\t            c => result.push(c),\n298\t        }\n299\t    }\n300\t    result\n301\t}\n302\t\n303\t/// Inline CSS for HTML output (~3KB budget)\n304\tconst CSS: &str = r#\"\n305\t:root {\n306\t  --bg: #ffffff;\n307\t  --fg: #1a1a1a;\n308\t  // Conversation\n    html.push_str(\"<div class=\\\"conversation\\\">\\n\");\n\n    for event in events {\n        let role_class = match event.role {\n            Role::User => \"user\",\n            Role::Assistant => \"assistant\",\n            Role::System => \"system\",\n            Role::ToolCall => \"tool-call\",\n            Role::ToolResult => \"tool-result\",\n        };\n\n     html.push_str(\"</div>\\n\"); // turn\n    }\n\n    html.push_str(\"</div>\\n\"); // conversation\n\n    // Footer\n    html.push_str(\"<footer>\\n\");\n    html.push_str(\"<div Render a session as structured Markdown\npub fn render_markdown(events: &[Event], meta: &SessionManifest) -> Result<String> {\n    let mut md = String::new();\n\n    // YAML frontmatter\n    md.push_str(\"---\\n\");\n    md.push_str(&format!(\"session_id: {}\\n\", meta.session_id));\n    md.push_str(&format!(\"source_agent: {}\\n\", meta.source_agent));\n    if let Some(ref project) = meta.project {\n        md.push_str(&format!(\"project: {}\\n\", project));\n    }\n    md.push_str(&format!(\"started: {}\\n\", meta.started.to_rfc3339()));\n    if let Some(ref ended) = meta.ended {\n        md.push_str(&format!(\"ended: {}\\n\", ended.to_rfc3339()));\n    }\n    md.push_str(&format!(\"turns: {}\\n\", meta.turns));\n    if let Some(ref outcome) = meta.outcome {\n        md.push_str(&format!(\"outcome: {}\\n\", outcome));\n    }\n    if !meta.files_touched.is_empty() {\n        md.push_str(\"files_touched:\\n\");\n        for file in &meta.files_touched {\n            md.push_str(&format!(\"  - {}\\n\", file));\n        }\n    }\n    if let Some(ref model) = meta.model {\n        md.push_str(&format!(\"model: {}\\n\", model));\n    }\n    md.push_str(\"---\\n\\n\");\n\n    // Summary if available\n    if let Some(ref summary) = meta.summary {\n        md.push_str(&format!(\"**Summary:** {}\\n\\n\", summary));\n    }\n\n    // Conversation\n    for event in events {\n        let role_label = match event.role {\n            Role::User => \"**User**\",\n            Role::Assistant => \"**Assistant**\",\n            Role::System => \"**System**\",\n            Role::ToolCall => \"**Tool Call**\",\n            Role::ToolResult => \"**Tool Result**\",\n        };\n\n        md.push_str(&format!(\n            \"{} ({})\\n\\n\",\n            role_label,\n            format_timestamp(&event.ts)\n        ));\n\n        if let Some(ref tool) = event.tool {\n            md.push_str(&format!(\"*Tool: {}*\\n\\n\", tool));\n        }\n\n        // Render content with code blocks preserved\n        md.push_str(&render_content_markdown(&event.content));\n        md.push_str(\"\\n\\n---\\n\\n\");\n    }\n\n    Ok(md)\n}\n\n/// Render content with code block detection for HTML\nfn render_content_html(content: &str) -> String {\n    let mut result = String::new();\n    let mut pos = 0;\n\n    // Detect code blocks: ```lang ... ```\n    while let Some(fence_start) = content[pos..].find(\"```\") {\n        // Add text before fence\n        let before_fence = &content[pos..pos + fence_start];\n        result.push_str(&escape_html(before_fence));\n\n        pos += fence_start + 3;\n\n        // Extract language (rest of line)\n        let lang_end = content[pos..].find('\\n').unwrap_or(content[pos..].len());\n        let lang = &content[pos..pos + lang_end];\n        let lang = lang.trim();\n\n        pos += lang_end + 1; // Skip newline\n\n        // Find closing fence\n        if let Some(fence_end) = content[pos..].find(\"```\") {\n            let code = &content[pos..pos + fence_end];\n\n            result.push_str(\"<pre><code class=\\\"language-\");\n            result.push_str(&escape_html(lang));\n            result.push_str(\"\\\">\");\n            result.push_str(&escape_html(code));\n            result.push_str(\"</code></pre>\");\n\n            pos += fence_end + 3;\n\n            // Skip trailing newline\n            if pos < content.len() && content.as_bytes()[pos] == b'\\n' {\n                pos += 1;\n            }\n        } else {\n            // No closing fence, treat rest as text\n            result.push_str(\"<pre>\");\n            result.push_str(&escape_html(&content[pos..]));\n            result.push_str(\"</pre>\");\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Add remaining text\n    if pos < content.len() {\n        result.push_str(&escape_html(&content[pos..]));\n    }\n\n    result\n}\n\n/// Render content with code block detection for Markdown\nfn render_content_markdown(content: &str) -> String {\n    // For Markdown, we mostly preserve the original formatting\n    // Just ensure newlines are handled correctly\n    content.to_string()\n}\n\n/// Format duration between start and end\nfn format_duration(start: DateTime<Utc>, end: Option<DateTime<Utc>>) -> String {\n    let end = end.unwrap_or_else(Utc::now);\n    let duration = end.signed_duration_since(start);\n\n    let mut parts: Vec<String> = Vec::new();\n\n    if duration.num_days() > 0 {\n        parts.push(format!(\"{}d\", duration.num_days()));\n    }\n    if duration.num_hours() % 24 > 0 {\n        parts.push(format!(\"{}h\", duration.num_hours() % 24));\n    }\n    if duration.num_minutes() % 60 > 0 {\n        parts.push(format!(\"{}m\", duration.num_minutes() % 60));\n    }\n\n    if parts.is_empty() {\n        \"<1m\".to_string()\n    } else {\n        parts.join(\" \")\n    }\n}\n\n/// Format model(s) used\nfn format_models(model: Option<&str>) -> String {\n    model.unwrap_or(\"unknown\").to_string()\n}\n\n/// Format timestamp for display\nfn format_timestamp(ts: &DateTime<Utc>) -> String {\n    ts.format(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S UTC\").to_string()\n}\n\n/// Get role badge label\nfn role_badge_label(role: &Role) -> &'static str {\n    match role {\n        Role::User => \"User\",\n        Role::Assistant => \"Assistant\",\n        Role::System => \"System\",\n        Role::ToolCall => \"Tool\",\n        Role::ToolResult => \"Result\",\n    }\n}\n\n/// Escape HTML special characters\nfn escape_html(s: &str) -> String {\n    let mut result = String::with_capacity(s.len());\n    for c in s.chars() {\n        match c {\n            '&' => result.push_str(\"&amp;\"),\n            '<' => result.push_str(\"&lt;\"),\n            '>' => result.push_str(\"&gt;\"),\n            '\"' => result.push_str(\"&quot;\"),\n            '\\'' => result.push_str(\"&#x27;\"),\n            c => result.push(c),\n        }\n    }\n    result\n}\n\n/// Inline CSS for HTML output (~3KB budget)\nconst CSS: &str = r#\"\n:root {\n  --bg: #ffffff;\n  --fg: #1a1a1a;\n  --border: #e0e0e0;\n  --header-bg: #f5f5f5;\n  --code-bg: #f8f8f8;\n --tool-bg: #1e5f3e;\n    --tool-result-bg: #5f1e3e;\n  }\n}\n\n* { box-sizing: border-box; }\n\nbody {\n  margin: 0;\n  padding: 0;\n  font-family: 'SF Mono', 'Monaco', 'Inconsolata', 'Fira Mono', build_query(&searcher, &fields, &fuzzy_opts, &schema)?;\n        top_docs = searcher\n            .search(&fallback_query, &TopDocs::with_limit(fetch_limit))\n            .map_err(|e| {\n                AgentScribeError::DataDir(format!(\"Fuzzy fallback search failed: {}\", e))\n            })?;\n        if !top_docs.is_empty() {\n            used_fuzzy_fallback = true;\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Apply offset\n    let top_docs: Vec<_> = top_docs.into_iter().skip(opts.offset).collect();\n\n    // When token_budget is set, convert all fetched candidates so the knapsack\n    // can select optimally; otherwise cap at max_results.\n    let result_limit = if opts.token_budget.is_some() {\n        fetch_limit\n    } else {\n        opts.max_results\n    };\n\n    // Convert to SearchResult\n    let mut results: Vec<SearchResult> = Vec::new();\n    for (score, doc_addr) in &top_docs {\n        if results.len() >= result_limit {\n            break;\n        }\n        if let Some(result) = doc_to_search_result(&searcher, &fields, *doc_addr, *score, opts) {\n            results.push(result);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Apply sort order\n    apply_sort(&mut results, opts.sort);\n\n    // Apply token budget if specified\n    if let Some(budget) = opts.token_budget {\n        results = knapsack_pack(results, budget);\n    }\n\n    let elapsed = start.elapsed();\n search options.\nfn build_query(\n    searcher: &Searcher,\n    fields: &IndexFields,\n    opts: &SearchOptions,\n    _schema: &tantivy::schema::Schema,\n) -> Result<Box<dyn Query>> {\n    // Validate that at least one search mode or filter is specified\n    if opts.query.is_none()\n        && opts.error_pattern.is_none()\n        && opts.code_query.is_none()\n        && opts.like_session.is_none()\n        && opts.file_path.is_none()\n        && opts.git_commit.is_none()\n    {\n        return Err(AgentScribeError::DataDir(\n            \"No search query provided. Use <query>, --error, --code, --like, or a filter.\"\n                .to_string(),\n        ));\n    }\n\n    let mut clauses: Vec<(Occur, Box<dyn Query>)> = Vec::new();\n\n    // Main text query\n build_fulltext_query(searcher, fields, query_str)?\n        };\n        clauses.push((Occur::Must, query));\n    }\n\n    // Error fingerprint lookup\n    if let Some(ref error_pat) = opts.error_pattern {\n        let term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.error_fingerprint, error_pat);\n        let query = Box::new(FuzzyTermQuery::new(term, 1, true));\n        clauses.push((Occur::Must, query));\n    }\n\n    // Code search\n    if let Some(ref code_q) = opts.code_query {\n        let text_query = if opts.fuzzy {\n            build_fuzzy_query_for_field(fields.code_content, code_q, opts.fuzzy_distance)?\n        } else {\n            let (parsed, _errors) =\n                tantivy::query::QueryParser::for_index(searcher.index(), vec![fields.code_content])\n                    .parse_query_lenient(code_q);\n            Box::new(parsed)\n        };\n        clauses.push((Occur::Must, text_query));\n\n        // Filter to code_artifact doc_type if searching code\n        let doc_term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.doc_type, \"code_artifact\");\n        clauses.push((\n            Occur::Must,\n            Box::new(TermQuery::new(\n                doc_term,\n                tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n            )),\n        ));\n\n        // Language filter\n        if let Some(ref lang) = opts.code_lang {\n            let lang_term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.code_language, lang);\n            clauses.push((\n                Occur::Must,\n                Box::new(TermQuery::new(\n                    lang_term,\n                    tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n                )),\n            ));\n        }\n    } else if opts.doc_type_filter.is_none() {\n        // Default: only return session documents (never mix with code_artifacts)\n        let doc_term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.doc_type, \"session\");\n        clauses.push((\n            Occur::Must,\n field\n    if opts.solution_only {\n        let query_str = opts.query.as_deref().unwrap_or(\"\");\n        if !query_str.is_empty() {\n            let (parsed, _errors) = tantivy::query::QueryParser::for_index(\n                searcher.index(),\n                vec![fields.solution_summary],\n            )\n            .parse_query_lenient(query_str);\n            clauses.push((Occur::Should, Box::new(parsed)));\n        }\n    }\n\n    // --like <session-id>: find sessions with similar content (TF-IDF based MLT)\n    if let Some(ref like_id) = opts.like_session {\n        let mlt_query = build_more_like_this(searcher, fields, like_id)?;\n        clauses.push((Occur::Must, mlt_query));\n        // Exclude the source session from results\n        let exclude_term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.session_id, like_id);\n        clauses.push((\n            Occur::MustNot,\n            Box::new(TermQuery::new(\n &opts.agent {\n        let term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.source_agent, agent_name);\n        clauses.push((\n            Occur::Must,\n            Box::new(TermQuery::new(\n                term,\n                tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n            )),\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Project filter\n    if let Some(ref project) = opts.project {\n        let     Bound::Unbounded,\n        );\n        clauses.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(range)));\n    }\n\n    if let Some(before) = opts.before {\n        let tantivy_before = TantivyDateTime::from_timestamp_secs(before.timestamp());\n        let range = RangeQuery::new_date_bounds(\n            \"timestamp\".to_string(),\n            Bound::Unbounded,\n            Bound::Excluded(tantivy_before),\n        );\n        clauses.push((Occur::Must, Box::new(range)));\n    }\n\n    // Tag filter (AND logic - all tags must be present)\n    for tag in &opts.tag {\n tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n            )),\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Outcome filter\n    if let Some(ref outcome) = opts.outcome {\n        let term = tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n            )),\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Doc type filter\n    if let Some(ref dt) = opts.doc_type_filter {\n        let term = tantivy::schema::Term::from_field_text(fields.doc_type, dt);\n        clauses.push((\n            Occur::Must,\n            Box::new(TermQuery::new(\n                term,\n                tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n            )),\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Model filter\n    if let Some(ref model) = opts.model {\n        let term = tantivy::schema::IndexRecordOption::Basic,\n            )),\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // File path filter (exact term match on stored file_paths values)\n    if let Some(ref fp) = opts.file_path {\n
